The super power makes the vehicles run more quickly, the super cleaning function &nbsp;prevents the production of sediment piston which guarantees &nbsp;the lubrication system of no sludge and carbon deposition, bright and clean as ever, excellent soot control ability effectively reduces the soot oil pollution and abrasion, extends oil life, the excellent anti-abrasion and anti-oxidation capacity, even under bad working conditions can also provides excellent lubrication protection and prolong the service life of the engine, the good low-temperature fluidity can reduce start-up time and abrasion, it also saves the fuel, &nbsp;it has a good compatibility with EGR and SCR, it also plays a very important role in &nbsp;protecting rear exhaust treatment system, reducing harmful gas emissions and protecting the environment.<br />\r\n	<strong>适用范围：</strong>适用所有进口和国产高速四冲程重负荷涡轮增压国Ⅲ、国Ⅳ和欧Ⅳ液化气、天然气及柴油车，特别适用于采用EGR、SCR尾排处理装置的各种国产、进口液化气、天然气以及柴油发动机驱动的载重车型发动机润滑。<br />\r\n	<strong>注意事项：&nbsp;
